GT Equivalence Verification (CRK5)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) + c1*_f*A**c2
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is a fixed function of **A only** (no t-dependence):
\[
f(A)=0.5229500625821207\,A^{1/3}-0.3254156367450257\,A^{1/2}.
\]
So any matching candidate must (i) be independent of \(t\) after parameter choices, and (ii) equal a linear combination of exactly the two power terms \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\) with those fixed coefficients, for all \(A\) (on the common real domain).

---

### 1. \(A c0 + A^{c1}c2 + \frac{A^{c3}c4}{A^{c3}+c5}\)
Can set \(c0=0\). The rational term cannot become a pure power \(A^{1/2}\) or \(A^{1/3}\) for all \(A\) unless it is identically 0 (e.g., \(c4=0\)) or a constant (e.g., \(c5=0\Rightarrow c4\)). Either way you can’t produce both required powers with correct coefficients. **No.**

### 2. Sum of several terms all divided by \((A^{c0}+c2)\) plus \(A c3\) plus constant \(c9\)
To remove denominators for all \(A\), you’d need numerators arranged to cancel, but structure yields rational functions in \(A^{c0}\), not a sum of two distinct pure powers \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\). Setting denominator-related coefficients to 0 reduces to linear-in-\(A\) plus constant, not GT. **No.**

### 3. \(A c0 + A c1\max(0,-A+c2)+A c3 e^{c4 t}+ c5 e^{A c6}\sin(c7 t+c8)\)
To match GT must remove all \(t\)-dependence: set \(c3=0\) and \(c5=0\). Then remaining terms are piecewise-linear in \(A\), not fractional powers. **No.**

### 4. \(\frac{A c0}{A+c1}+A^{c2}c3 e^{c4 t}+A^{c5}c6 e^{c7 t}+ \frac{c8 t}{c9+t^2}\)
Remove \(t\): set \(c3=0,c6=0,c8=0\). Left with \(\frac{A c0}{A+c1}\), a rational function, not \(A^{1/3}-A^{1/2}\). **No.**

### 5. Linear/piecewise + \(\frac{A^{c4}c5}{A^{c4}+c6}\) + constants + \(\log(c9 t+1)\)
Must kill \(t\): set \(c8=0\). Remaining terms are linear/piecewise plus a bounded rational-in-\(A^{c4}\) term; cannot equal two fractional power terms for all \(A\). **No.**

### 6. \(A c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3 e^{c4 t}\)
Kill \(t\): \(c3=0\). Then only one power term \(A^{c1}\) plus linear \(A\). Cannot produce both \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\). **No.**

### 7. \(A c0 + c1 + \frac{c2}{c3+t}+ c4 e^{A c5}\sin(c6 t+c7)+ c8\max(0,A)\)
Kill \(t\): need \(c2=0\) and \(c4=0\). Left with linear in \(A\) plus constant and ReLU(A), not fractional powers. **No.**

### 8. \(\frac{A c0}{A+c1}+A c2 e^{c3 t}+A^{c4}c5 e^{c6 t}+\frac{c7}{c8+t}+c9\)
Kill \(t\): set \(c2=0,c5=0,c7=0\). Left rational + constant, not GT. **No.**

### 9. Linear/piecewise + \(e^{A c4}\sin(\cdot)\) + \(c7\log(c8|A|+1)\)
Kill \(t\): set \(c3=0\). Still has linear/piecewise and log(|A|+1), not a sum of two pure powers. **No.**

### 10. Many terms all divided by \((A^{1/4}+c1)\)
Any nonzero \(c1\) gives a non-power rational form. If \(c1=0\), denominator is \(A^{1/4}\) and each term becomes a power of \(A\):  
- \(A^{5/4}c0/A^{1/4}=c0 A\)  
- \(A^{1/4}A^{c2}c3/A^{1/4}=c3 A^{c2}\)  
- \(A^{1/4}c4/A^{1/4}=c4\) (constant), similarly \(c5\)  
- \(A c6/A^{1/4}=c6 A^{3/4}\)  
- \(A^{c2}c7/A^{1/4}=c7 A^{c2-1/4}\)  
- \(c8/A^{1/4}=c8 A^{-1/4}\)
You could set unwanted coefficients to 0, but you only get at most two adjustable exponents via \(c2\) and \(c2-1/4\), which differ by exactly \(1/4\). GT needs exponents \(1/3\) and \(1/2\) whose difference is \(1/6\), not \(1/4\). No way to make the two surviving powers be exactly \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\) simultaneously. **No.**

### 11. \(A^{c0}c1 e^{c2 t}+A^{c3}c4+\frac{c5}{c6+t}\)
Kill \(t\): set \(c2=0\) and \(c5=0\). Then \(c1 A^{c0}+c4 A^{c3}\). This can match GT by choosing:
- \(c0=\tfrac13,\; c1=0.5229500625821207\)
- \(c3=\tfrac12,\; c4=-0.3254156367450257\)
This yields exactly \(0.52295 A^{1/3}-0.325416 A^{1/2}\) for all \(A\) (on the shared real domain). **Yes.**

### 12. Rational-in-A terms + \(t\)-dependent terms
To kill \(t\): set \(c5=0,c7=0,c9=0\). Remaining is \(\frac{A c0}{A+c1}+\frac{A c2}{A+c3}+A c4+\frac{c5}{c6+t}\) (but \(c5\) already 0). This is rational/linear, not two fractional powers. **No.**

### 13–14. \(A c0|A|^{c1} + \frac{A c2}{A+c3\text{ or }c3+|A|} + \frac{c4 t}{c5+t^2} + c6|A|^{c1}\)
Kill \(t\): set \(c4=0\). Remaining involves \(|A|^{c1}\) and rational terms; also \(A|A|^{c1}= \text{sign}(A)|A|^{c1+1}\), not a pure \(A^{1/3}\) over reals, and you still can’t get both \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\) cleanly without absolute/sign issues. **No.**

### 15. \(\frac{A c0}{A+c1}+A^{c2}c3(c4+t)^{c5}+\frac{c6}{c7+t}+c8\)
Kill \(t\): need \(c3=0\) and \(c6=0\). Left rational + constant, not GT. **No.**

### 16. \(A c0 + \frac{A c1}{A+c2} + c3/A^5\)
No way to form \(A^{1/3}\) and \(A^{1/2}\). **No.**

### 17. Linear/piecewise + \(\frac{A c4}{(A c5+1)^2}+A c6 e^{c7 t}+c8\)
Kill \(t\): set \(c6=0\). Remaining is linear/piecewise plus rational, not fractional powers. **No.**

### 18. \(A c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3 t + c4 + c5\log(c6 e^{c7 t}+1)\)
Kill \(t\): set \(c3=0,c5=0\). Left \(A c0 + c2 A^{c1}+c4\): only one fractional power plus linear/constant. **No.**

### 19. \(A c0 + A^{c1}c2 + A^{c3}c4 e^{c5 t}+A^{c6}c7 e^{c8 t}+c9\)
Kill \(t\): set \(c4=0,c7=0\) (or \(c5=c8=0\) but then still extra powers). Then reduces to \(A c0 + c2 A^{c1}+c9\): cannot get two needed powers. **No.**

### 20. Purely \(t\)-based rational + cosine(log(...))
No \(A^{1/3}\) or \(A^{1/2}\) structure. **No.**

### 21. \(A c0 + c1\frac{t}{c2+t^2}+ c3|A|^{c4}+c5|A|^{c6}\)
Kill \(t\): set \(c1=0\). Then linear in \(A\) plus absolute-power terms; cannot represent \(A^{1/3}\) and \(-A^{1/2}\) as pure powers of \(A\) over reals without absolute/sign mismatch, and also the linear term must vanish (set \(c0=0\)), leaving \(|A|^{c4},|A|^{c6}\) not \(A^{1/3},A^{1/2}\). **No.**

### 22–23. Absolute-power terms + \(t\)-rational + log(...)
Even killing \(t\) and log terms, you get \(|A|^{c1}\) and \(A|A|^{c1}\) forms, not the required pure powers of \(A\). **No.**

### 24. \(c0/(c1+t)+ c2\sin(c3\log(c4|A|+1)+c5)\)
Not a sum of power laws. **No.**

### 27. \(A^{c0}c1 e^{c2 t}+ c3\frac{t}{c4+t^2}\)

Kill \(t\): set \(c4=0\). Left rational + linear, not GT. **No.**

### 31. \(A c0 + \frac{c1}{c2+t} + \frac{c3 e^{c4|A|}}{c2+t} + \frac{c5 t e^{c4|A|}}{c2+t} + c6 e^{c7\sin(Ac8+c9)}\)

Let me check: with c2=0, c9=0, and setting various c's to 0, we get A^(1-c0)·c1 + A·c3 + A^(1-c0)·c4 + A^c5·c6 + c7 + A^(c5-c0)·c8.
